			}

				mission = GER_viability_of_the_coalition
				days = 25
			}			
		}

			factor = 500
		}

	GER_toggle_hiddenburg_program = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		days_remove = 17
		cost = 25
		days_re_enable = 50
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		available = {
			has_idea = GER_idea_hindenburg_programme
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_the_hindenburg_program
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_idea_hindenburg_programme
				}
				remove_ideas = GER_idea_hindenburg_programme
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = GER_civilian_government_vs_ohl
					value = -0.1
					tooltip_side = GER_balance_civilian
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = GER_idea_hindenburg_programme
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = GER_civilian_government_vs_ohl
					value = -.1
					tooltip_side = GER_balance_ohl
				}
			}
			
		}
	}

GER_great_war = {

	#unrestricted submarine warfare bonus
	GER_intensification_of_submarine_warfare = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_human_torpedo
		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = GER_unrestricted_submarine_warfare_flag
				has_completed_focus = GER_unrestricted_submarine_warfare
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
			has_war = yes
			NOT = {
				has_idea = GER_unrestricted_submarine_warfare_idea4
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		remove_effect = {
			#increase the submarine warfare
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_intensification_of_submarine_warfare_tooltip
			GER_intensification_of_submarine_warfare_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = GER_restricted_submarine_warfare_increased_once
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_war = no
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = USA
				}
				has_country_flag = GER_restricted_submarine_warfare_increased_once
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	GER_send_zimmermann_telegram = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = zimmermann_telegram_intercepted
				any_other_country = {
					has_country_flag = mexico_agrees
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				has_war_with_major = no
				is_in_faction_with = USA
				has_war_together_with = USA
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with = USA
				has_country_flag = GER_send_zimmermann_telegram_possible
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
				has_war_together_with = FROM
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				original_tag = MEX
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_zimmermann_depesche_tt
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_germany.53
					days = 1
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = zimmermann_telegram
			custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_tt
			effect_tooltip = {
				GER = {
					add_to_faction = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_war = no
		}
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				ENG = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
							OR = {
								is_ai = no
								has_completed_focus = ENG_room_40
								has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_decryption_boost
							}
						}	
						country_event = ww1_england.9				
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 500
			modifier = {
				longest_war_length < 40
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

		days_mission_timeout = 365
		days_re_enable = 1
		selectable_mission = no
		is_good = no
		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}

					remove_idea = GER_idea_national_debt
					add_idea = GER_idea_national_debt_2
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = GER_idea_national_debt_2
					}

						add_idea = GER_idea_national_debt_3
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = GER_idea_national_debt_3
						}
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = GER_idea_national_debt_3
							add_idea = GER_idea_national_debt_4
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
		}
		complete_effect = {
		}

	GER_decision_frustration_among_general_staff = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		days_mission_timeout = 410
		is_good = no
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			tag = GER
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				NOT = {
					has_idea = GER_famine
				}
				has_war_support > 0.65
			}
		}
		activation = {
			#at war with Britain and another major
			#So russia + UK trigger, as well as USA + UK
			any_enemy_country = {
				NOT = {
					tag = ENG
				}
				is_major = yes
				has_capitulated = no
			}
			ENG = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
			has_war_support < 0.5
			OR = {
				has_war_support < 0.2
				has_idea = GER_famine
			}
			longest_war_length > 36
			enemies_naval_strength_ratio > 0.85
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = exasperation_mission_done
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			set_country_flag = exasperation_mission_done
			activate_decision = GER_decision_naval_order_of_october_1918
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germanrework.149
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}

	#trigger kiel mutinies if war support is too low
	GER_decision_naval_order_of_october_1918 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		days_remove = 180
		is_good = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_completed_focus = GER_heeringens_plan
				}
				has_war = yes
				longest_war_length > 30
			}
			else = {
				has_war_with_major = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
			has_country_flag = exasperation_mission_done
		}
		available = {
			has_war_with_major = yes
			enemies_naval_strength_ratio > 0.85
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 9.9
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_10
		days_remove = 10
		remove_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = GER_all_or_nothing_plan
				days = 180
			}	
		}
		complete_effect = {
			add_command_power = -10
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_war_support < 0.4
						has_idea = GER_famine
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_germany.11
						days = 7
					}
				}
			}		
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = kiel_mutiny
				has_war = no
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				date < 1918.08.20
			}
		}
	}

	GER_fleet_in_being_mission = {
		days_mission_timeout = 1096
		selectable_mission = no
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}
		activation = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_the_fleet_in_being
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GER_fleet_in_being_mission_done
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = get_36_battleships
				check_variable = {
					num_ships_with_type@battleship > 35
				}
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05
			set_country_flag = GER_fleet_in_being_mission_done
		}
		complete_effect = {
			# These effects are dogshit, considering building 36 battleships is a huge task
			add_war_support = 0.1
			navy_experience = 25
			set_country_flag = GER_fleet_in_being_mission_done
		}
		
	}

	# SCHLIFFEN PLAN
	##################
	GER_schliffen = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_draw_up_staff_plans
		available = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_schlieffen_plan_enacted }
			FRA = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = neutrality_idea
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				NOT = {				
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			tag = GER
			NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_schlieffen_plan_enacted }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GER_schliffenmoltkeplan
			}
		}		
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
	    	original_tag = GER
		}
		days_remove = 5
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = BEL
			}
		}
		war_with_on_remove = BEL
		war_with_on_remove = LUX
		war_with_on_remove = HOL
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				is_on_continent = europe
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = BEL
					is_owned_by = LUX
					is_owned_by = HOL
					state = 29
					state = 33
					state = 785
					state = 865
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			BEL = {
				country_event = ww1_belgium.70
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 793
						state = 42
						state = 51
					}
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = GER_schliffen_preparations
					days = 25
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = GER_schlieffen_plan_enacted
				ENG = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = ENG_idea_not_ready_yet }
						remove_ideas = ENG_idea_not_ready_yet
					}
				}
			}
			GER = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						HOL = {
							NOT = {
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = HOL
						type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					}
					add_state_claim = 1063
				}
			}
			GER = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { 
							BEL = { has_war_with = ROOT }
							has_country_flag = BEL_submit_to_GER_1914
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = BEL
						type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					}
					add_state_claim = 906
					add_state_claim = 907
					hidden_effect = {
						news_event = kis_news.130
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						LUX = {
							exists = yes
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
								has_war_with = FRA
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							}	
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = LUX
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}	
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_more_aggressive_schlieffen_plan
					}
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = GER_schlieffen_plan2
						days = 60
					}
					else = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = GER_schlieffen_plan
							days = 60
						}
					}
				}
				
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 10
					name = GER_schliffenmoltkeplan
				}
				
				add_state_claim = 8
			}	
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10000
		}
	}

	# LUDENDORFF OFFENSIVE
	###########################
	GER_ludendorff_offensive = { # This should be turned into an event - Shall
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_draw_up_staff_plans
		available = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			NOT = {
				FRA = {
					has_capitulated = yes 
				}
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_country_flag = great_war_winner
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
				has_war_with = RUS
			}
			# shouldn't able to launch this early
			OR = {
				has_idea =  GER_famine
				has_war_support < 0.5
				has_stability < 0.5
				surrender_progress > 0.05
			}
		}	
		visible = {
			tag = GER
			has_global_flag = great_war
			NOT = {
				has_active_mission = before_the_leaves_fall
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}	
			# has_completed_focus = GER_oberster_kriegsherr
			has_completed_focus = GER_organise_fresh_offensives
			# You can't launch Ludendorff Offensive without him
			has_character = GER_erich_ludendorff
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		days_remove = 120
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = FRA
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
				FRA = {
					has_capitulated = yes 
				}
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_country_flag = great_war_winner
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
				controls_state = 16
				16 = { is_controlled_by = PREV }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_ludendorff_offensive_tt
			add_ideas = GER_idea_ludendorff_offensive
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = ludendorff_offensive
				news_event = {
					id = ww1_germany.92
					hours = 3
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			# It would be critical for the German Empire
			add_war_support = -0.10
			add_stability = -0.10
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = GER_idea_ludendorff_offensive
				set_global_flag = ludendorff_offensive_failed
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = idea_mass_desertion }
					}
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = idea_mass_desertion
						days = 90
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = GER_idea_ludendorff_offensive
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = GER_erich_ludendorff
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					GER_erich_ludendorff = {
						is_hired_as_advisor = yes
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_war_with = USA
					date > 1918.3.21
					# Near Paris
					controls_province = 9561
					controls_province = 11518
				}
			}
		}
	}

		available = {
			# has_completed_focus = GER_atlantic_class
			has_completed_focus = GER_v_thirty_production
			is_subject = no
			has_capitulated = no
			has_war_with = ENG
			num_of_naval_factories > 10
			any_controlled_state = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				is_coastal = yes
			}
			OR = {
				has_tech = early_submarine
				has_tech = early_ship_hull_submarine
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 70
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
				create_ship = {
					type = ship_hull_submarine_1
					creator = GER
					equipment_variant = "U Class"
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_ship = {
					type = submarine_1
					creator = GER
					equipment_variant = "U Class"
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				# By 1917, it had 140 and the U-boats had destroyed about 30 percent of the world's merchant ships.
				has_navy_size = {
					size > 200
					type = submarine
				}
			}
		}
	}
	GER_stricten_rationing = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		days_remove = 50
		cost = 25
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_introduce_rationing_measures
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_introduce_rationing_measures
			NOT = {
				has_idea = GER_idea_extreme_rationing
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = GER_1916_food_strikes
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_germanrework.155
						days = 3
					}
					set_country_flag = GER_1916_food_strikes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_idea_light_rationing
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_idea_light_rationing
					add_idea = GER_idea_moderate_rationing
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer_early
					}
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = GER_mission_famine_timer_early
						days = 50
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
					}
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
						days = 50
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_idea_moderate_rationing
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_idea_moderate_rationing
					add_idea = GER_idea_strict_rationing
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer_early
					}
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = GER_mission_famine_timer_early
						days = 60
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
					}
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
						days = 60
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_idea_strict_rationing
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_idea_strict_rationing
					add_idea = GER_idea_extreme_rationing
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer_early
					}
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = GER_mission_famine_timer_early
						days = 70
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_active_mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
					}
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = GER_mission_famine_timer
						days = 70
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = GER_1916_food_strikes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	# great war in short timer
	before_the_leaves_fall = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_blackshirt_march
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 75
		activation = {
			has_global_flag = great_war
			GER = { has_war_with = FRA }
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation_alone
				has_global_flag = before_the_leaves_fall_flag
				has_global_flag = before_the_leaves_fall_failed
			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = before_the_leaves_fall_tt
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FRA = { has_war = no }
						GER = { has_war = no }
					}
					has_global_flag = great_war_ends
					has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
					has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
					has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation_alone
					has_global_flag = before_the_leaves_fall_flag
					has_global_flag = before_the_leaves_fall_failed
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = great_war
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = no
		timeout_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = FRA
							has_war_with = GER
							has_war_together_with = GER
							has_war_together_with = FRA
						}
					}
					add_war_support = -0.05
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = before_the_leaves_fall_failed
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_war_with = FRA
							has_war_with = GER
							has_war_together_with = GER
							has_war_together_with = FRA
						}
					}
					add_war_support = -0.05
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GER = {
							not = {
								has_completed_focus = GER_heeringens_plan
							}
						}
					}
					GER = {
						complete_national_focus = GER_schlieffen_plan_scuppered
						country_event = ww1_germanrework.46 #Removes Moltke due to stroke
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = before_the_leaves_fall_flag
		}
	}
}

GER_agadir_crisis = {
	GER_agadir_crisis_opportunity = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = agadir_crisis
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
		}
		priority = 50
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 150
		activation = {
			has_global_flag = agadir_crisis
			has_war = no
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
				has_global_flag = great_war
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			set_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
			custom_effect_tooltip = agadir_crisis_end
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -75
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_news_triggered
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = SPR
							tag = FRA
							tag = ENG
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_morocco.27
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_morocco.15
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	GER_instant_react_to_agadir = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = agadir_crisis
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = FRA_MOR_french_victory
				has_global_flag = FRA_MOR_moroccan_victory
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
				has_war_with = FRA
				FRA = {
					has_war_with = MOR
				}
			}
			has_crisis = no
		}
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			has_capitulated = no
			NOT = {
				has_idea = GER_financial_crisis_of_agadir
				has_idea = GER_financial_crisis_of_agadir_2
			}
		}
		days_remove = 10
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				is_subject = yes
				has_capitulated = yes
				has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
				FRA = {
					has_war_with = MOR
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 25
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			#custom_effect_tooltip = GER_instant_react_to_agadir_tt
			#add_political_power = -100
			
		}
		remove_effect = {
			FRA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_morocco.6
					days = 2
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_morocco.17
					days = 50
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_sms_panther_morocco
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 5
				name = GER_moroccan_crisis
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				has_global_flag = GER_reaction_time
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	GER_retire_from_morocco = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}
		activation = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = GER_financial_crisis_of_agadir
				has_idea = GER_financial_crisis_of_agadir_2
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = agadir_crisis
			has_country_flag = GER_sms_panther_morocco
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
				has_war_with = FRA
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 35
		is_good = no
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
			}
			has_country_flag = GER_sms_panther_morocco
		}
		selectable_mission = yes
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				is_subject = yes
				has_capitulated = yes
				has_global_flag = agadir_crisis_ends
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_sms_panther_morocco
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				GER = {
					country_event = {
						id = ww1_morocco.17
						days = 20
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = GER_sms_panther_morocco
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = FRA
						tag = SPR
						tag = ENG
						tag = GER
					}
					has_war = no
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_morocco.24
					days = 2
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_morocco.24
					days = 2
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_morocco.26
				days = 3
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = wait_25_days
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	GER_help_white_russia = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = AUS
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_war = no
			has_war_support > 0.5
			has_stability > 0.5
			has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
			is_faction_leader = yes
			# if = {
			# 	limit = {
			# 		tag = GER
			# 	}
			# 	has_completed_focus = GER_reichspakt
			# }
		}
		visible = {
			has_russian_civil_war = yes
			has_country_flag = great_war_winner
			is_greater_germany = yes
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 250
		days_remove = 10
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = SOV
			}
		}
		#war_with_on_remove = SOV
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 10
				name = GER_help_white_russia
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SOV
				type = topple_government
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
					OR = {
						is_subject_of = SOV
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
				}
				PREV = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = topple_government
					}
				}
			}
			BLR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction = no
						is_neighbor_of = SOV
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = PREV
							AND = {
								any_other_country = {
									is_neighbor_of = PREV
									OR = {
										is_in_faction_with = PREV.PREV
										is_subject_of = PREV.PREV
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					PREV = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = PREV
							type = puppet_wargoal_focus
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	GER_help_nationalist_france = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = AUS
			}
		}
		available = {
			any_country = {
				has_country_flag = FRA_socialist_france_flag
				any_country = {
					has_country_flag = FRA_nationalist_france_flag
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}
			has_war = no
			is_subject = no
			has_war_support > 0.5
			has_stability > 0.5
			has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
			is_faction_leader = yes
			# if = {
			# 	limit = {
			# 		tag = GER
			# 	}
			# 	has_completed_focus = GER_reichspakt
			# }
		}
		visible = {
			any_country = {
				has_country_flag = FRA_socialist_france_flag
				any_country = {
					has_country_flag = FRA_nationalist_france_flag
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = great_war_winner
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = AUS
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = GER }
				OR = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = GER_confederation
					has_cosmetic_tag = GER_HRE			
					has_cosmetic_tag = AUH_HRE				    
				}
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 400
		days_remove = 10
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				original_tag = FRA
				has_country_flag = FRA_socialist_france_flag
			}
		}
		#war_with_on_remove = FRC
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.2
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 10
				name = GER_help_nationalist_france
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FRC
				type = topple_government
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				SOV = { exists = no }
				add = 100
			}
		}
	}
}
GER_decision_military_advisers = {
	GER_advisors_FROM = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_army_support
		available = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_manpower > 999
			FROM = {
				has_war = yes
				NOT = { has_idea = GER_idea_german_military_advisors } 
			}
		}	
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				NOT = {
					original_tag = TUR
					capital_scope = { 
						OR = {
							is_on_continent = africa
							is_on_continent = middle_east 
						}	
					}
				} 

			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_support_triple_alliance_armies
		}		
		fire_only_once = no
		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}
		days_remove = 25
		remove_effect = {
			add_manpower = -1000
			FROM = { add_timed_idea = { idea = GER_idea_german_military_advisors days = 360 } }
		}
		cost = 75
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { has_war = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_manpower < 30000
			}
		}
	}
}

prestigious_projects = {
	GER_decision_mittelafrika = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_operation
		allowed = { tag = GER }
		available = {
			has_war = no
			has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = GAB
					is_core_of = RCG
					is_core_of = COG
					is_core_of = ZAM
					is_core_of = MLW
					iS_core_of = UGA
					is_core_of = KEN
					is_core_of = RWA
					is_core_of = CHA
					is_core_of = GHA
					is_core_of = IVO
					state = 789
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			is_subject = no
			# has_completed_focus = GER_claim_mittelafrika
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = GAB
					is_core_of = RCG
					is_core_of = COG
					is_core_of = ZAM
					is_core_of = MLW
					iS_core_of = UGA
					is_core_of = KEN
					is_core_of = RWA
					is_core_of = CHA
					is_core_of = GHA
					is_core_of = IVO
					state = 789
				}
			}
			MAF = { exists = no }
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
		}
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 50
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_war = yes
					is_subject = yes
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = GAB
								is_core_of = RCG
								is_core_of = COG
								is_core_of = ZAM
								is_core_of = MLW

								is_core_of = IVO
								state = 789
							}
						}
					}
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			add_political_power = 90
		}
		remove_effect = {
			country_event = ww1_germany.26
		}
	}
	GER_decision_expand_mittelafrika = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_operation
		allowed = { tag = GER }
		target_trigger = {

				tag = MAF
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_war = no
			has_subject = MAF
			has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
			OR = {
				any_owned_state = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = MAF
					}
					OR = {
						region = 140
						region = 184
						region = 185
						region = 215

						region = 224

				has_subject = TZN

				has_subject = LIB
				has_subject = KEN #Kenya Revolt :(
			}
		}
		visible = {
			is_subject = no
			has_subject = MAF
			NOT = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
			OR = {
				any_owned_state = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = MAF
					}
					OR = {
						region = 140
						region = 184
						region = 185
						region = 215
						region = 217
						region = 223
						region = 224
						region = 226
						region = 227
						state = 902 #West Nile
						state = 903 #Zanzibar

						state = 1142
						state = 769
					}
				}
				has_subject = TOG
				has_subject = NMB
				has_subject = TZN
				has_subject = CMR
				has_subject = LIB
				has_subject = KEN #Kenya Revolt :(
			}
			# has_completed_focus = GER_claim_mittelafrika
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_war = yes
					is_subject = yes
					NOT = { has_subject = MAF }
					has_government = communism
				}
			}	
		}	
		cancel_effect = {
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		cost = 30
		days_remove = 20
		days_re_enable = 50
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		remove_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = MAF
					}
					OR = {
						region = 140
						region = 184
						region = 185
						region = 215
						region = 217
						region = 223
						region = 224
						region = 226
						region = 227
						state = 902 #West Nile
						state = 903 #Zanzibar
						state = 660
						state = 1142
						state = 769
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = MAF
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							# Togoland
							state = 777
							state = 794
							# Kamerun
							state = 539
							state = 769
							state = 813
							state = 814
							state = 1143
							state = 815
							state = 1144
							# Ostafrika
							state = 546
							state = 768
							# Sdwestafrika
							state = 541
							state = 1050
						}
					}
					add_core_of = MAF
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = GER
					OR = {
						tag = TOG
						tag = NMB
						tag = TZN
						tag = CMR
						tag = KEN
						tag = LIB
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_on_continent = africa
							is_core_of = PREV
						}
						transfer_state_to = MAF
						if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									# Togoland
									state = 777
									state = 794
									# Kamerun
									state = 539
									state = 769
									state = 813
									state = 814
									state = 1143
									state = 815
									state = 1144
									# Ostafrika
									state = 546
									state = 768
									# Sdwestafrika
									state = 541
								}
							}
							add_core_of = MAF
						}
					}
					every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = MAF }
				}
				MAF = { 
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						 transfer_troops = yes
					} 
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					MAF = {
						owns_state = 546
						546 = {
							is_capital = no
						}
					}
				}
				MAF = {
					set_capital = { state = 546 }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				MAF = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = GHA
								is_core_of = NGA
								is_core_of = KEN
							}
						}
						set_demilitarized_zone = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ETH = { is_neighbor_of = PREV }
							GER = { owns_state = 268 }
						}
						ETH = {
							give_military_access = GER
							give_military_access = PREV
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								AFA = {
									exists = yes
									NOT = {
										has_war_with = GER
										has_war_with = PREV
									}
								}
							}
							AFA = {
								give_military_access = GER
								give_military_access = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	GER_annex_new_east_prussia = {
		icon = generic_operation
		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				OR = {
					owns_state = 87
					owns_state = 98
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
			is_subject = no
			owns_state = 5
			owns_state = 85
			87 = {
				is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
			}
			98 = {
				is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
			87 = {
				OWNER = {
					controls_state = PREV
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			98 = {
				OWNER = {
					controls_state = PREV
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 75
		complete_effect = {
			87 = {
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				add_resistance = 20
			}
			98 = {
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
				add_resistance = 20
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_government = fascism }
				has_stability < 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

GER_afghan_expeditions = {
	GER_niedermayerhentig_recruit = {
		icon = generic_operation
		allowed = { tag = GER }
		fire_only_once = yes
		available = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AFG }
		}
		visible = {
			always = no
			# OR = {
			# 	has_war_with = RUS
			# 	has_war_with = RAJ
			# }
			# AFG = {
	 		# 	NOT = {
			# 		has_war_with = ROOT
			# 		has_country_flag =  GER_niedermayer_hentig_recruited
			# 	} 
			# }
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = { tag = AFG }
		}
		cost = 10
		days_remove = 10
		remove_effect = {
			AFG = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_afghanistan.2
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	GER_ottoman_allow_afg = {
		icon = generic_operation
		cost = 30
		allowed = { tag = GER }
		fire_only_once = yes
		available = {
			is_in_faction_with = TUR
			has_war_with = ENG
			has_war_with = RAJ
			AFG = {
				exists = yes
				has_war = no
				has_country_flag = GER_expedition_start
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				is_in_faction_with = AFG
				NOT = {
					TUR = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
					has_war_with = ENG
					has_war_with = RAJ
				}
				AFG = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = great_war_ends }
			has_war_with = ENG
			has_war_with = RAJ
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AFG }
			TUR = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			AFG = {
				exists = yes
				has_war = no
				has_country_flag = GER_niedermayer_hentig_recruited
				has_country_flag = GER_expedition_start
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			army_experience = 10
			add_command_power = 20
			TUR = {
				add_command_power = 20
				add_political_power = 25
			}
		}
		days_remove = 10
	}
	GER_begin_afghan_expedition = {
		icon = generic_operation
		allowed = { tag = GER }
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AFG }
			has_war_with = ENG
			has_war_with = RAJ
			NOT = { has_global_flag = great_war_ends }
			AFG = {
				exists = yes
				has_war = no
				has_country_flag = GER_niedermayer_hentig_recruited
				NOT = { has_country_flag =  GER_expedition_start } 
			}
		}
		cost = 35
		available = {
			has_war_with = ENG
			has_war_with = RAJ
			NOT = { has_global_flag = great_war_ends }
			has_manpower > 500
			AFG = {
				exists = yes
				has_war = no
				has_country_flag = GER_niedermayer_hentig_recruited
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				is_in_faction_with = AFG
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ENG
					has_war_with = RAJ	
				}
				AFG = {
					OR = {
						exists = no
						has_war = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_germany.78
				days = 30
			}
			add_manpower = -500
			hidden_effect = {
				AFG = {
					set_country_flag = GER_expedition_start
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 10
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

							has_idea = idea_great_depression
							has_war_with = FRA
						}
						FRA = {
							is_subject = no
						}
					}
					FRA = {
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_germany.143
							days = 10
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { 
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				OR = {
					has_government = communism
					has_government = fascism
					has_country_leader_ideology = absolute_monarchy
					has_country_leader_ideology = semi_constitutional_monarchy
				}
				has_civil_war = no
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FRA
					ratio > 1.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_idea = idea_great_depression
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				any_other_country = {
					is_constituent_of_germany = no
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	GER_interwar_invite_in_reichspakt = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_ally_imperialist_coup
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = AUS
			}
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = BUL
					tag = POL
					tag = UKR
					tag = IRE
					tag = FIN
					tag = EST
					tag = LAT
					tag = COU
					tag = UBD
					tag = LIT
					tag = SCO
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
					has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				}
				is_subject = no
				is_in_faction = no
				has_war = no
			}
		}
		available = {
			FROM = {
				has_war = no							
			}		
		}
		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = GER
					# has_completed_focus = GER_reichspakt
				}
				is_greater_germany = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			has_country_flag = great_war_winner
			is_faction_leader = yes
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 25
		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_ai = yes
							OR = {
								tag = LIT
								tag = UBD
								tag = BLR
								tag = UKR
								tag = POL
								tag = FIN
							}
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = ROOT
							value = 200
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_historical_focus_on = no
							is_ai = yes
						}
						random_list = {
							4 = {
								add_ai_strategy = {
									type = alliance
									id = ROOT
									value = 200
								}
							}
							6 = {
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = generic.5
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 85
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						tag = LIT
						tag = UBD
						tag = BLR
						tag = UKR
						tag = POL
						tag = FIN
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

economy_decisions = {
	GER_restore_schantung_bahn_control = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_railway

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_china_or_warlord_no_tt = yes
				NOT = {
					gives_military_access_to = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					controls_state = 597
					controls_state = 872
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = great_war_winner
					NOT = { has_global_flag = CHI_join_great_war }
				}
				owns_state = 745
				controls_state = 745
				is_subject = no
				has_capitulated = no
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					OR = {
						AND = {
							owns_state = 597
							controls_state = 597
						}
						AND = {
							owns_state = 872
							controls_state = 872
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		days_remove = 5

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				give_military_access = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

	GER_law_on_the_constitution_for_alsace_bund = {
		cost = 10
		visible = {
			tag = GER
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_debug = yes
					has_country_flag = GER_show_debug_decisions
				}
				has_country_flag = GER_constitution_for_alsace_unlocked_in_bund
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GER_started_voting_bundesrat
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = GER_has_majority_in_bund
				has_majority_in_bundesrat = yes
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GER_started_voting_bundesrat
		}
		days_remove = 30
        ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_majority_in_bundesrat = yes }
				clr_country_flag = GER_constitution_for_alsace_unlocked_in_bund
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_likely_to_pass
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_if_law_passes_bund
				GER_alsace_lorraine_constitution_effect = yes

				GER_remove_all_swayed_states = yes

				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_if_law_fails_bund
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_stability = -0.1
					add_political_power = -75
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_law_alsace_new_member_passed_in_bundesrat
				else = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = GER_likely_to_be_rejected
					custom_effect_tooltip = GER_if_law_passes_bund
					effect_tooltip = {
						GER_alsace_lorraine_constitution_effect = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = GER_if_law_fails_bund
					add_stability = -0.1
					add_political_power = -75

					GER_remove_all_swayed_states = yes
				}
			}
			GER_remove_voting_stuff = yes
		}
	}

GER_reichstag_category = {

	GER_toggle_debug_decisions = {
		available = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			is_debug = yes
		}
		complete_effect = {
